[30;1m29 | [0m[35mfollowing the same rules as Python source code: put a backslash[0m
[30;1m30 | [0m[35m(``\``) at the end of all lines except the last line. However, if[0m

[30;1m32 | [0m[35mdon't need the backslash.[0m
